NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, AR. RAJU, Biological son of Sri. V. Arunachalam, born on 5th June 1964 residing at Old No. 2/20, New No. 2/23,
MR. PL. House, S.P.K. Street, Konapet, Tirumayam Taluk, Pudukkottai-622 503, by way of this Public Notice, inform that
Late Sri.Mr. Palaniappa Chettiar and Smt. Annapoorani Achi had legally adopted me as their son on 14th November, 1986
by way of Registered Deed bearing No.33/1986 on the Sub-RegistrarвЂ™s Office, Tirumayam, Pudukottai District. My adopted
father Sri. Mr. Palaniappa Chettiar (late) passed away on 16-08-1974 and Smt. Annapoorani Achi has passed away on
25-11-1999. Hence hereinafter I shall be known as PL. MURUGAPPAN.
AR. RAJU.
Konapet, 6th November 2015.
